<h1 id="helm-基于曲率混合专家的超几何大语言模型研究解读">HELM: 基于曲率混合专家的超几何大语言模型研究解读</h1>
<h2 id="研究目标与实际意义">研究目标与实际意义</h2>
<h3 id="研究目标">研究目标</h3>
<ul>
<li>开发完全在<strong>超几何空间</strong>运行的大语言模型(LLM)，以更好地匹配自然语言固有的语义层次和几何结构</li>
<li>解决现有超几何Transformer模型的三大主要缺点：表示空间不灵活、缺乏必要操作组件和可扩展性差</li>
<li>创建首个十亿参数级别的全超几何大语言模型，并验证其在推理和泛化能力方面的优势</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="实际问题与意义">实际问题与意义</h3>
<ul>
<li>当前大语言模型主要在欧几里得空间运行，这与文本数据的内在结构存在潜在不匹配</li>
<li>语言模型中的词元(token)嵌入显示出非欧几里得几何特性，尤其表现为负曲率分布，意味着存在层次结构</li>
<li>不尊重词元嵌入的基础几何结构会导致训练不稳定和生成能力下降，而超几何空间能够自然表达层次关系</li>
<li>超几何空间具有容量扩展、尺度自由和低扭曲等特性，为词元提供了更合适的"呼吸空间"</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="方法创新与技术细节">方法创新与技术细节</h2>
<h3 id="超几何几何基础：lorentz模型">超几何几何基础：Lorentz模型</h3>
<p>论文使用Lorentz模型作为超几何空间的实现方式：</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>n维Lorentz模型</strong>定义为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>L</mi><mi>K</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>K</mi></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(L^n_K, g^K_n)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.11666em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.275331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>，其中：</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>L</mi><mi>K</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>:</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>x</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L^n_K = \{x \in \mathbb{R}^{n+1} : \langle x,x \rangle_L = 1/K, x_t &gt; 0\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.958661em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.814108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>K</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mtext>diag</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^K_n = \text{diag}(-1,1,...,1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08833em; <li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">K &lt; 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72243em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>是常数负曲率</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Lorentz内积</strong>：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><msub><mi>y</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>x</mi><mi>s</mi><mi>T</mi></msubsup><msub><mi>y</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>x</mi><mi>T</mi></msup><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>K</mi></msubsup><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\langle x,y \rangle_L = -x_t y_t + x^T_s y_s = x^T g^K_n y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span>，其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是时间维度，<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_s</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是空间维度</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>切空间</strong>：点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msubsup><mi>L</mi><mi>K</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \in L^n_K</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.958661em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.275331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>处的切空间定义为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>x</mi></msub><msubsup><mi>L</mi><mi>K</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>:</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">T_x L^n_K = \{y \in \mathbb{R}^{n+1} : \langle x,y \rangle_L = 0\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.958661em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">x</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.275331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.814108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="曲率混合专家模型mice">曲率混合专家模型(MICE)</h3>
<p>为解决现有超几何Transformer模型表示空间不灵活的问题，论文提出了<strong>曲率混合专家</strong>(Mixture-of-Curvature Experts)：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>多曲率空间</strong>：每个专家在不同曲率的超几何流形上运行，允许模型编码更精细的文本几何结构</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>网络结构</strong>：对于输入词元<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>L</mi><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_t \in L^{K,n}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6891em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.280556em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.841331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>，MICE模块的工作流程为：</p>
<ul>
<li>计算门控分数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_{t,i}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.716668em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>，确定哪些路由专家被激活</li>
<li>将词元投影到专家的曲率空间：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mrow><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msub><mi>K</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow></msqrt><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">s_{t,i} = \sqrt{K/K_{s,i}}x_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.716668em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">s</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.24em; vertical-align: -0.323054em;"></span><span class="mord sqrt"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.916946em;"><span class="svg-align" style="top: -3.2em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.2em;"></span><span class="mord" style="padding-left: 1em;"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <li>通过专家处理投影的词元</li>
<li>将处理结果投影回输入曲率空间：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mrow><msub><mi>K</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi></mrow></msqrt><mi>H</mi><mi>F</mi><mi>F</mi><msub><mi>N</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>s</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y_{t,i} = \sqrt{K_{s,i}/K}HFFN_{s,i}(s_{t,i})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.716668em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <li>
<p><strong>数学表达</strong>：</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>C</mi><msubsup><mi>E</mi><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>r</mi></msub><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><msub><mo>⊕</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mfrac><mrow><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></munderover><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>r</mi></msub></munderover><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><msqrt><mrow><mo>−</mo><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></munderover><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>r</mi></msub></munderover><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>L</mi></msub></mrow></msqrt></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> MiCE^{N_s}_{N_r}(x_t) = x_t \oplus_L \left(\frac{\sum^{N_s}_{i=1} y_{t,i} + \sum^{N_r}_{i=1} z_{t,i}}{\sqrt{-K||\sum^{N_s}_{i=1} y_{t,i} + \sum^{N_r}_{i=1} z_{t,i}||_L}}\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.31686em; </li>
</ol>
<h3 id="超几何多头潜在注意力hmla">超几何多头潜在注意力(HMLA)</h3>
<p>为解决超几何模型的可扩展性问题，论文提出了<strong>超几何多头潜在注意力</strong>：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>目的</strong>：减少KV缓存大小和训练中的活跃内存需求</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>机制</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>将词元投影到潜在查询和键值向量：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>c</mi><mi>t</mi><mi>Q</mi></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c^Q_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.20499em; vertical-align: -0.245756em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.959239em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.45424em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">Q</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.245756em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>和<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>c</mi><mi>t</mi><mrow><mi>K</mi><mi>V</mi></mrow></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c^{KV}_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08833em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>将潜在向量向上投影为多头查询、键和值</li>
<li>实现解耦的HOPE方案，通过超几何线性变换生成额外查询向量和共享键</li>
<li>使用Lorentz连接合并向量，并通过超几何自注意力计算最终输出</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>优势</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>推理时只需缓存潜在键值对，内存占用为O((n_kv+n_r)L)</li>
<li>传统超几何自注意力需要O(2nn_hL)的内存，而HMLA通过选择n_kv,n_r ≪ nn_h显著降低内存需求</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="超几何旋转位置编码hope">超几何旋转位置编码(HOPE)</h3>
<p>论文设计了<strong>超几何旋转位置编码</strong>以匹配现代大语言模型：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>数学定义</strong>：对于第i个词元：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>H</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>P</mi><mi>E</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msqrt><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Θ</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>s</mi></msub><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi></mrow></msqrt><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Θ</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>s</mi></msub><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
HoPE(z_i) = \left[\sqrt{\|R_{i,\Theta}(z_i)_s\|^2 - 1/K}, R_{i,\Theta}(z_i)_s\right]
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">Ho</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">PE</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.04398em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.40003em; margin-left: -0.04398em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Θ</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{i,\Theta}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.00773em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mtight">Θ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是旋转矩阵，作用于词元空间维度</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>理论性质</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>有效性</strong>：HOPE只编码相对位置信息</li>
<li><strong>长期衰减</strong>：随相对位置增加，注意力分数衰减</li>
<li><strong>对任意词元距离的鲁棒性</strong>：可以在任意相对距离上达到最大值</li>
<li><strong>位置注意力模式</strong>：可以学习对角线或非对角线注意力模式</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="超几何rms标准化hyperbolic-rmsnorm">超几何RMS标准化(Hyperbolic RMSNorm)</h3>
<p>论文实现了<strong>超几何RMS标准化</strong>，定义为：<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>M</mi><mi>S</mi><mi>N</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>r</mi><msub><mi>m</mi><mi>L</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msqrt><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>M</mi><mi>S</mi><mi>N</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>m</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi></mrow></msqrt><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>R</mi><mi>M</mi><mi>S</mi><mi>N</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>m</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><msup><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mi>T</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
RMSNorm_L(x) = [\sqrt{\|RMSNorm(x_s)\| - 1/K}, RMSNorm(x_s)]^T
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">RMSN</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">or</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.24em; vertical-align: -0.256125em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord sqrt"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.983875em;"><span class="svg-align" style="top: -3.2em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.2em;"></span><span class="mord" style="padding-left: 1em;"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">RMSN</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">or</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord">1/</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.94388em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.2em;"></span><span class="hide-tail" style="min-width: 1.02em; height: 1.28em;"><svg width="400em" height="1.28em" viewBox="0 0 400000 1296" preserveAspectRatio="xMinYMin slice"><path d="M263,681c0.7,0,18,39.7,52,119
c34,79.3,68.167,158.7,102.5,238c34.3,79.3,51.8,119.3,52.5,120

M1001 80h400000v40h-400000z"></path></svg></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.256125em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">RMSN</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">or</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.891331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中RMSNorm是欧几里得RMS标准化。这个设计保持了输入缩放不变性，增强了梯度稳定性和鲁棒性。</p>
<h3 id="完整helm架构">完整HELM架构</h3>
<p>论文提出两种HELM变体：</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>HELM-MICE</strong>：带有曲率混合专家的超几何LLM，每个专家在不同曲率空间工作</li>
<li><strong>HELM-D</strong>：密集型超几何LLM，类似于经典的仅解码器架构</li>
</ol>
<p>整体架构包含以下组件：</p>
<ul>
<li>超几何词嵌入层</li>
<li>一系列超几何解码器块，每个包含：
<ul>
<li>注意力组件(HMLA或超几何自注意力)</li>
<li>FFN组件(MICE或HFFN)</li>
<li>超几何RMS标准化和残差连接</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>最后一层投影到logits进行下一个词元预测</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="实验验证与结果">实验验证与结果</h2>
<h3 id="实验设置">实验设置</h3>
<p>实验评估了HELM变体在两个参数规模下的性能：</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>小型模型</strong>：~1亿参数</li>
<li><strong>大型模型</strong>：~10亿参数</li>
</ul>
<p>训练数据:</p>
<ul>
<li>Wikipedia英文数据集(~6.4M行文本，约5B词元)</li>
<li>使用LLaMA3.1-8B分词器(词表大小128K)</li>
</ul>
<p>对照模型:</p>
<ul>
<li>密集型欧几里得模型：LLaMA</li>
<li>稀疏型欧几里得模型：DeepSeekV3</li>
</ul>
<p>评估任务:</p>
<ul>
<li>STEM和一般知识推理：MMLU、ARC-Challenging和OpenbookQA</li>
<li>常识推理：CommonsenseQA和HellaSwag</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="主要实验结果">主要实验结果</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>HELM模型与欧几里得模型对比</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>1亿参数HELM-D在5个测试中有4个超过LLaMA</li>
<li>1亿参数HELM-MICE在所有5个测试中超过DeepSeekV3</li>
<li>10亿参数HELM-MICE在所有测试中超过DeepSeekV3，总体准确率更高</li>
<li>HELM模型在更困难的推理基准(MMLU和ARC-Challenging)上表现尤其出色</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>平均准确率对比</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>1亿参数HELM-D: 24.0% vs LLaMA: 23.3%</li>
<li>1亿参数HELM-MICE: 24.2% vs DeepSeekV3: 22.8%</li>
<li>10亿参数HELM-MICE: 24.9% vs DeepSeekV3: 23.9%</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>曲率混合与固定曲率对比</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>进行了消融实验，比较HELM-MICE(可变曲率)与MICE-CONST(固定曲率)</li>
<li>HELM-MICE在5个测试中的4个中表现更好</li>
<li>即使是固定曲率的MICE-CONST也在所有测试中优于欧几里得模型</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="消融实验">消融实验</h3>
<p>论文还进行了额外的消融研究：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>HMLA vs 超几何多头自注意力</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>HELM-MICE在5个任务中的3个优于使用标准超几何自注意力的变体</li>
<li>两种超几何模型都优于欧几里得模型</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>HOPE vs 学习式相对位置编码</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>HELM-MICE在5个任务中的4个优于使用学习式位置编码的变体</li>
<li>在ARC-Challenging基准上，学习式位置编码表现更好，可能因为与非均匀编码的推理提示更好地对齐</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="未来研究方向与挑战">未来研究方向与挑战</h2>
<h3 id="值得探索的问题">值得探索的问题</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何大语言模型的缩放规律：研究计算资源和数据规模如何影响超几何LLM的性能</li>
<li>非欧几里得几何在更复杂任务(如数学推理)中的适用性</li>
<li>多种几何空间(超几何、球形、欧几里得)的混合模型，以更好匹配不同类型的语言结构</li>
<li>更深入研究词元嵌入空间的曲率分布与语义信息的关系</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="技术机会">技术机会</h3>
<ul>
<li>开发适用于超几何空间的更高效优化方法，减少训练时间(目前HELM训练时间是欧几里得模型的1.5-1.8倍)</li>
<li>设计新的超几何注意力机制，进一步提高内存效率</li>
<li>探索超几何几何与其他先进技术(如量化、蒸馏)的结合</li>
<li>将超几何表示学习扩展到多模态大模型中</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="不足与局限性">不足与局限性</h2>
<h3 id="论文存在的局限">论文存在的局限</h3>
<ul>
<li>受计算资源限制，实验仅比较了在相同5B词元上训练的模型，而未与商用大规模预训练LLM比较</li>
<li>仅使用维基百科数据集，可能导致模型在某些领域(如数学推理)的经验不足</li>
<li>未深入分析不同任务类型对超几何表示需求的差异</li>
<li>超几何模型的训练时间明显长于欧几里得模型(1.5-1.8倍)，在计算效率方面仍有改进空间</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="需要进一步验证的问题">需要进一步验证的问题</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何空间是否适合所有类型的语言模型任务，还是仅适合特定类型的推理任务</li>
<li>随着模型规模和数据量增加，超几何与欧几里得模型的性能差距是否会扩大或缩小</li>
<li>HELM架构在多语言环境中的表现如何，不同语言可能具有不同的层次结构特性</li>
<li>超几何表示对长文本建模和长距离依赖的影响</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="实用创新与应用启示">实用创新与应用启示</h2>
<h3 id="值得学习的创新点">值得学习的创新点</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>曲率混合专家(MICE)</strong>：允许不同专家在不同曲率空间工作，实现更精细的几何结构编码</li>
<li><strong>超几何多头潜在注意力(HMLA)</strong>：通过潜在空间压缩实现内存高效的超几何注意力</li>
<li><strong>超几何旋转位置编码(HOPE)</strong>：为超几何空间设计的位置编码，保持了RoPE的理论性质</li>
<li><strong>超几何RMS标准化</strong>：为超几何模型提供梯度稳定性和鲁棒性</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="实用启示">实用启示</h3>
<ul>
<li>在构建语言模型时，考虑数据的内在几何结构可能带来性能提升，特别是对于包含复杂层次关系的数据</li>
<li>混合曲率模型比单一曲率模型更具表达能力，能够捕获更丰富的语义关系</li>
<li>超几何模型在复杂推理任务上表现尤其出色，可考虑在特定领域应用中采用</li>
<li>即使在计算资源有限的情况下，小型超几何模型也可能比同等规模的欧几里得模型表现更好</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="需要补充的背景知识">需要补充的背景知识</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何几何的基本概念，包括Lorentz模型、Poincaré球模型等不同表示方法</li>
<li>语言模型中的位置编码技术，特别是旋转位置编码(RoPE)的工作原理</li>
<li>混合专家(MoE)架构在大语言模型中的应用</li>
<li>Ricci曲率等几何度量及其在机器学习中的应用</li>
</ul>
<p>HELM通过将超几何几何与大语言模型相结合，为语言模型研究提供了一个新的视角。这种方法不仅理论上更符合语言的内在结构，实验结果也表明它能带来实际的性能提升，特别是在复杂推理任务上。随着技术进一步成熟，这种方法可能会对下一代语言模型的设计产生重要影响。</p>
<h1 id="理解在超几何空间中微调clip用于开放词汇语义分割">理解在超几何空间中微调CLIP用于开放词汇语义分割</h1>
<h2 id="研究目标与实际意义-1">研究目标与实际意义</h2>
<h3 id="研究目标-1">研究目标</h3>
<ul>
<li>从<strong>层次对齐</strong>的角度解释为何同时微调CLIP的文本编码器和图像编码器能显著提升开放词汇语义分割性能</li>
<li>利用超几何空间的自然层次表示能力，解释微调过程中文本嵌入的层次级别变化</li>
<li>设计一种可解释、参数高效的微调策略，使CLIP获得分割能力的同时保持其泛化能力</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="实际问题与意义-1">实际问题与意义</h3>
<ul>
<li>开放词汇语义分割旨在开发能为图像中每个像素用开放类别集合标注的分割模型</li>
<li>CLIP等视觉-语言基础模型通常用于提供开放词汇识别能力，但它们原本是基于图像级监督训练的</li>
<li>当前方法在如何微调CLIP上存在争议：冻结文本编码器以保持强大文本嵌入能力，或同时微调两个编码器以获得更好的分割性能</li>
<li>了解微调如何影响CLIP表示的层次结构，对开发更有效的微调策略具有重要意义</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="方法创新与技术细节-1">方法创新与技术细节</h2>
<h3 id="超几何空间背景">超几何空间背景</h3>
<p>论文使用<strong>Poincaré球模型</strong>来表示超几何空间，该模型能够自然地表达层次结构：</p>
<ul>
<li>具有半径1/√c和负曲率-c (c &gt; 0)的Poincaré球模型定义为：<br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>:</mo><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D}^n_c := \{x \in \mathbb{R}^n : c\|x\|&lt;1\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.93033em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span>，具有度量<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><msubsup><mi>λ</mi><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></msubsup><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>E</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^{\mathcal{D}}_c = \lambda^2_{c,x}g^E</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08833em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.22444em; vertical-align: -0.383108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">x</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.383108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.841331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; <li>超几何半径：定义为点到超几何空间中心的距离，表示层次级别<br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi><mi>a</mi><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>x</mi></msub><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>d</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mi>c</mi></msub></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mfrac><mn>2</mn><msqrt><mi>c</mi></msqrt></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>t</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>n</mi><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msqrt><mi>c</mi></msqrt><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Rad_x := d_{\mathcal{D}_c}(x,0) = (\frac{2}{\sqrt{c}})tanh^{-1}(\sqrt{c}\|x\|)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">x</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0001em; vertical-align: -0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <li>中心附近的点（较小半径）对应低层级视觉嵌入（如像素级），边缘附近的点（较大半径）对应高层级视觉嵌入（如图像级）</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="关键发现：微调clip时的超几何半径变化">关键发现：微调CLIP时的超几何半径变化</h3>
<p>研究者发现，微调过程中CLIP文本嵌入的超几何半径会发生变化：</p>
<ul>
<li>微调前，文本嵌入具有较大的超几何半径（接近边缘）</li>
<li>微调后，文本嵌入的超几何半径变小（向中心移动）</li>
<li>这表明微调过程调整了文本嵌入的层次级别，使其与像素级层次结构对齐，从而赋予CLIP分割能力</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="hyperclip方法">HyperCLIP方法</h3>
<p>基于上述发现，作者提出了HyperCLIP，一种在超几何空间中微调CLIP的策略：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>超几何半径调整</strong>：通过缩放变换直接调整CLIP嵌入的超几何半径</p>
<ul>
<li>使用分块对角缩放矩阵<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mi>K</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S = diag(S_1, S_2, ..., S_K)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ia</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">...</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>，其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>S</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>×</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S_k \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times n}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.05764em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.771331em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.771331em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mbin mtight">×</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>通过调整块大小n，可以在简单的对角缩放(n=1)和任意变换(n=d)之间平衡</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>微调过程</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>将特征嵌入z映射到超几何空间：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>e</mi><mi>x</mi><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>0</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">exp^{\mathcal{D},c}_0(z)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.22555em; vertical-align: -0.266308em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.959239em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.43369em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.266308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>应用Möbius矩阵乘法：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><msub><mo>⊗</mo><mi>c</mi></msub><mi>e</mi><mi>x</mi><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>0</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S \otimes_c exp^{\mathcal{D},c}_0(z)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin"><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.22555em; vertical-align: -0.266308em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.959239em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.43369em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.266308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>映射回欧几里得空间：<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>l</mi><mi>o</mi><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mn>0</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>S</mi><msub><mo>⊗</mo><mi>c</mi></msub><mi>e</mi><mi>x</mi><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>0</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>c</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">log^{\mathcal{D},c}_0(S \otimes_c exp^{\mathcal{D},c}_0(z))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.22555em; vertical-align: -0.266308em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.959239em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.43369em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.266308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin"><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.22555em; vertical-align: -0.266308em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.959239em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.43369em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.18091em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.266308em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">))</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>CLIP的原始组件保持冻结状态</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>理论支持</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>通过定理1证明缩放矩阵可以直接调整超几何半径</li>
<li>超几何半径随缩放参数变化满足单调性</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数复杂度</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>K-块对角矩阵的参数数量为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>d</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d^2/K</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span></span></span></span></span>，复杂度为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>d</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(d^2/K)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>可以通过共享块矩阵进一步减少参数量至<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>d</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mi>K</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(d^2/K^2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>设置n=1时，参数复杂度降至<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(d)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="实验验证与结果-1">实验验证与结果</h2>
<h3 id="实验设置-1">实验设置</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>数据集</strong>：
<ul>
<li>训练：COCO-Stuff数据集（约118,000张密集标注图像，171个语义类别）</li>
<li>测试：ADE20K(A-150,A-847)、PASCAL VOC(PAS-20,PAS-20b)、PASCAL-Context(PC-59,PC-459)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>评估指标</strong>：平均交并比(mIoU)</li>
<li><strong>实现细节</strong>：
<ul>
<li>基于Transformer的CLIP模型（ViT-B/16和ViT-L/14）</li>
<li>Adam优化器，学习率1×10<sup>-5，权重衰减10</sup>-4</li>
<li>在CLIP的每层自注意力模块中应用分块对角可学习权重</li>
<li>Poincaré球模型的曲率c设为0.01</li>
<li>训练80,000次迭代，使用4个NVIDIA A800 GPU</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="与现有方法对比">与现有方法对比</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>标准基准对比</strong>（表1）：</p>
<ul>
<li>HyperCLIP在六个测试集上都取得了最佳结果</li>
<li>与CAT-Seg相比，HyperCLIP在ViT-B/16上平均提高约1%，在ViT-L/14上平均提高约0.9%</li>
<li>与SAN相比（另一种参数高效微调方法），HyperCLIP在PC-459上提升6.6%，在PC-59上提升4.7%</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>效率比较</strong>（表5）：</p>
<ul>
<li>HyperCLIP仅需微调CLIP 5.6M参数（约4%），远少于其他方法</li>
<li>OVSeg: 147.2M，CAT-Seg: 39.5M，SAN: 8.4M</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>其他任务应用</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>开放词汇目标检测：在COCO数据集上取得26.3% AP^Base_50和42.7% AP^Novel_50</li>
<li>开放词汇全景分割：在ADE20K上取得29.2% PQ，超过ODISE、FC-CLIP和MAFT+</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="消融实验-1">消融实验</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>微调CLIP的编码器</strong>（表6）：</p>
<ul>
<li>同时微调文本和图像编码器效果最佳(12.3% on A-847)</li>
<li>仅微调文本编码器(11.1%)或仅微调图像编码器(10.3%)效果次之</li>
<li>与现有PEFT方法相比，HyperCLIP表现更好</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>对角块大小</strong>（表4）：</p>
<ul>
<li>随着块大小增加，性能在类别较少的数据集上逐渐提升</li>
<li>在类别较多的数据集上（如A-847），性能在块大小约128时达到饱和点</li>
<li>最佳性能在块大小128时实现（A-847: 12.3%, PC-459: 19.2%, A-150: 32.1%）</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>文本嵌入的超几何半径影响</strong>（图5）：</p>
<ul>
<li>初始超几何半径约为7.5</li>
<li>最佳性能在半径约为6.0时实现</li>
<li>偏离最佳半径值（增加或减少）都会导致性能下降</li>
<li>这表明特定视觉任务可能有相对固定的最佳超几何半径</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Möbius矩阵乘法的必要性</strong>（表7）：</p>
<ul>
<li>使用Möbius矩阵乘法的模型在所有数据集上表现更好</li>
<li>表明Möbius矩阵乘法对于最小化CLIP嵌入的超几何半径至关重要</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="未来研究方向与挑战-1">未来研究方向与挑战</h2>
<h3 id="值得探索的问题-1">值得探索的问题</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何半径作为量化视觉任务粒度的指标：研究结果表明，文本嵌入的超几何半径在不同数据集间保持相对固定，这可能意味着分割任务的粒度可以用超几何半径来量化</li>
<li>其他视觉-语言任务的层次对齐：探索不同视觉任务（如检测、分类、检索）是否需要不同的超几何半径</li>
<li>动态调整超几何半径：设计能根据输入自动调整超几何半径的方法</li>
<li>多模态表示学习中的超几何几何：进一步研究超几何空间在多模态表示学习中的应用</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="技术机会-1">技术机会</h3>
<ul>
<li>对不同视觉任务开发基于超几何半径的自动微调策略</li>
<li>将超几何学习应用于其他需要层次结构理解的领域，如视频理解、3D场景理解</li>
<li>开发更高效的超几何操作实现，进一步提高计算效率</li>
<li>结合其他参数高效微调技术，如LoRA、适配器等，设计更高效的超几何微调方法</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="不足与局限性-1">不足与局限性</h2>
<h3 id="论文存在的局限-1">论文存在的局限</h3>
<ul>
<li>主要关注CLIP模型，未探讨方法在其他视觉-语言模型上的适用性</li>
<li>虽然证明了超几何半径的重要性，但未深入研究不同类别所需的最优半径可能有所不同</li>
<li>论文中使用的Poincaré球模型是超几何空间的一种表示，其他模型（如Lorentz模型）可能有不同特性</li>
<li>计算效率方面的讨论较少，特别是超几何操作可能带来的额外计算开销</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="需要进一步验证的问题-1">需要进一步验证的问题</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何半径是否真的能完全量化视觉任务的粒度，或者这只是一个相关因素</li>
<li>方法在更多样的开放词汇任务上的泛化能力</li>
<li>超几何空间微调相比于其他微调方法的优势是否在更大规模的模型上依然存在</li>
<li>不同层次的视觉任务（像素级、区域级、图像级）是否确实对应于不同的超几何半径</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="实用创新与应用启示-1">实用创新与应用启示</h2>
<h3 id="值得学习的创新点-1">值得学习的创新点</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>超几何视角</strong>：通过超几何空间分析微调过程，揭示了文本嵌入层次级别变化的重要性</li>
<li><strong>参数高效微调</strong>：通过简单的缩放变换，仅使用少量参数就显著提升了模型性能</li>
<li><strong>可解释性</strong>：提供了微调改进性能的几何解释，使优化策略更加透明和可理解</li>
<li><strong>理论支撑</strong>：通过数学定理证明缩放矩阵对超几何半径的调整作用</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="实用启示-1">实用启示</h3>
<ul>
<li>在微调视觉-语言模型时，应考虑不同模态嵌入的层次对齐问题</li>
<li>参数高效微调不仅可以减少计算成本，还可以通过有针对性的修改提高性能</li>
<li>考虑数据的内在几何结构可能导致更有效的表示学习和微调策略</li>
<li>超几何空间为理解和操作层次结构提供了强大工具，可应用于多种计算机视觉任务</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="需要补充的背景知识-1">需要补充的背景知识</h3>
<ul>
<li>超几何几何基础知识，特别是Poincaré球模型和Möbius运算</li>
<li>视觉-语言模型（如CLIP）的架构和预训练方法</li>
<li>开放词汇语义分割任务的评估方法和挑战</li>
<li>参数高效微调技术（PEFT）的基本概念和方法</li>
</ul>
<p>HyperCLIP通过超几何空间的视角，不仅解释了为什么微调CLIP的文本编码器能提升开放词汇语义分割性能，还提供了一种参数高效的微调策略。这种方法通过直接调整超几何半径来改变嵌入的层次级别，从而使CLIP获得分割能力。更重要的是，研究揭示了超几何半径可能作为量化视觉任务粒度的指标，为未来研究提供了新的方向。</p>
<h1 id="通过潜在层次适配器学习进行细粒度视觉-语言模型微调">通过潜在层次适配器学习进行细粒度视觉-语言模型微调</h1>
<h2 id="研究目标与实际意义-2">研究目标与实际意义</h2>
<h3 id="研究目标-2">研究目标</h3>
<ul>
<li>开发一种新型的<strong>潜在层次适配器</strong>(Latent Hierarchical Adapter, LatHAdapter)用于视觉-语言模型(VLM)在少样本分类任务上的高效微调</li>
<li>通过学习下游训练数据的<strong>潜在语义层次结构</strong>，提供更丰富、更细粒度的指导来改进适配器学习过程</li>
<li>解决现有基于适配器方法在对齐视觉和文本表示时的两个主要局限性：无法捕捉类别与图像样本之间的一对多关联，以及难以建立未知类别与图像之间的准确关联</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="实际问题与意义-2">实际问题与意义</h3>
<ul>
<li>现有的适配器方法主要通过嵌入空间中的显式空间邻近性约束来学习/对齐文本-视觉模态，这种方法不适合建模类别与图像之间的层次化一对多关系</li>
<li>传统方法通常使用手工制作的文本提示或依靠大型语言模型生成的类别描述，限制了它们对未知类别的泛化能力</li>
<li>超几何空间的特性（如指数级体积增长）特别适合表示层次结构，可以更自然地建模类别、属性和图像样本之间的语义层次关系</li>
<li>所提出的方法作为一个即插即用(plug-and-play)方案，可以轻松集成到现有VLM微调框架中，以提高其性能</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="方法创新与技术细节-2">方法创新与技术细节</h2>
<h3 id="poincaré球模型基础">Poincaré球模型基础</h3>
<p>LatHAdapter采用<strong>Poincaré球模型</strong>作为超几何空间的表示方式：</p>
<ul>
<li>定义为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>D</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>D</mi></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(D^n_c, g^D)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09133em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>，其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>D</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>:</mo><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D^n_c = \{x \in \mathbb{R}^n: c\|x\| &lt; <li>曲率参数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c &gt;
